[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m

       [1m-c[22m, [1m--bytes[0m[m

[?1049h[?1h=GREP(1)                                        General Commands Manual                                        GREP(1)[m
[m
[1mNAME[0m[m
       grep, egrep, fgrep - print lines matching a pattern[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mgrep [22m[[4mOPTIONS[24m] [4mPATTERN[24m [[4mFILE[24m...][m
       [1mgrep [22m[[4mOPTIONS[24m] [1m-e [4m[22mPATTERN[24m ... [[4mFILE[24m...][m
       [1mgrep [22m[[4mOPTIONS[24m] [1m-f [4m[22mFILE[24m ... [[4mFILE[24m...][m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       [1mgrep  [22msearches  for  [4mPATTERN[24m  in  each  [4mFILE[24m.   A [4mFILE[24m of “[1m-[22m” stands for standard input.  If no [4mFILE[24m is given,[m
       recursive searches examine the working directory, and nonrecursive searches read standard input.  By  default,[m
       [1mgrep [22mprints the matching lines.[m
[m
       In  addition,  the  variant programs [1megrep [22mand [1mfgrep [22mare the same as [1mgrep -E [22mand [1mgrep -F[22m, respectively.  These[m
       variants are deprecated, but are provided for backward compatibility.[m
[m
[1mOPTIONS[0m[m
   [1mGeneric Program Information[0m[m
       [1m--help [22mOutput a usage message and exit.[m
[m
       [1m-V[22m, [1m--version[0m[m
              Output the version number of [1mgrep [22mand exit.[m
[m
   [1mMatcher Selection[0m[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K       [1m-E[22m, [1m--extended-regexp[0m[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 2 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              Interpret [4mPATTERN[24m as an extended regular expression (ERE, see below).[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 3 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 4 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K       [1m-F[22m, [1m--fixed-strings[0m[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 5 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              Interpret [4mPATTERN[24m as a list of fixed strings (instead of regular expressions), separated  by  newlines,[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 6 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              any of which is to be matched.[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 7 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 8 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K       [1m-G[22m, [1m--basic-regexp[0m[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 9 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              Interpret [4mPATTERN[24m as a basic regular expression (BRE, see below).  This is the default.[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 10 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 11 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K       [1m-P[22m, [1m--perl-regexp[0m[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 12 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              Interpret the pattern as a Perl-compatible regular expression (PCRE).  This is experimental and [1mgrep -P[0m[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 13 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              may warn of unimplemented features.[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 14 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 15 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K   [1mMatching Control[0m[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 16 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K       [1m-e [4m[22mPATTERN[24m, [1m--regexp=[4m[22mPATTERN[0m[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 17 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              Use [4mPATTERN[24m as the pattern.  If this option is used multiple times or is combined with the [1m-f  [22m([1m--file[22m)[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 18 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              option,  search  for  all  patterns given.  This option can be used to protect a pattern beginning with[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 19 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              “-”.[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 20 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 21 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K       [1m-f [4m[22mFILE[24m, [1m--file=[4m[22mFILE[0m[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 22 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              Obtain patterns from [4mFILE[24m, one per line.  If this option is used multiple times or is combined with the[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 23 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              [1m-e  [22m([1m--regexp[22m)  option,  search  for  all  patterns  given.  The empty file contains zero patterns, and[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 24 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              therefore matches nothing.[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 25 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K[HM              Output the version number of [1mgrep [22mand exit.[m
[27;1H[K[3m Manual page grep(1) line 24 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K[HM       [1m-V[22m, [1m--version[0m[m
[27;1H[K[3m Manual page grep(1) line 23 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              [1m-e  [22m([1m--regexp[22m)  option,  search  for  all  patterns  given.  The empty file contains zero patterns, and[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 24 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              therefore matches nothing.[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 25 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 26 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K       [1m-i[22m, [1m--ignore-case[0m[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 27 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              Ignore case distinctions, so that characters that differ only in case match each other.[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 28 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 29 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K       [1m-v[22m, [1m--invert-match[0m[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 30 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              Invert the sense of matching, to select non-matching lines.[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 31 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 32 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K       [1m-w[22m, [1m--word-regexp[0m[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 33 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              Select only those lines containing matches that form whole  words.   The  test  is  that  the  matching[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 34 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              substring must either be at the beginning of the line, or preceded by a non-word constituent character.[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 35 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              Similarly, it must be either at the end of the line or followed by a  non-word  constituent  character.[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 36 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              Word-constituent  characters  are letters, digits, and the underscore.  This option has no effect if [1m-x[0m[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 37 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              is also specified.[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 38 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 39 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K       [1m-x[22m, [1m--line-regexp[0m[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 40 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              Select only those matches that exactly match the whole line.  For a regular expression pattern, this is[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 41 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              like parenthesizing the pattern and then surrounding it with [1m^ [22mand [1m$[22m.[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 42 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 43 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K       [1m-y     [22mObsolete synonym for [1m-i[22m.[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 44 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 45 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K   [1mGeneral Output Control[0m[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 46 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K       [1m-c[22m, [1m--count[0m[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 47 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              Suppress  normal  output;  instead  print  a count of matching lines for each input file.  With the [1m-v[22m,[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 48 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              [1m--invert-match [22moption (see below), count non-matching lines.[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 49 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 50 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K       [1m--color[22m[[1m=[4m[22mWHEN[24m], [1m--colour[22m[[1m=[4m[22mWHEN[24m][m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 51 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              Surround the matched (non-empty) strings, matching lines, context lines, file names, line numbers, byte[m
[3m Manual page grep(1) line 52 (press h for help or q to quit)[23m[K[K              offsets,  and separators (for fields and groups of context lines) with escape sequences to display them[m
